   195	
   196	/// Compute a "qualified name" by prepending the namespace (joined with `__`) to the js_name.
   197	/// When there is no namespace, this returns the js_name unchanged.
   198	/// This is used to disambiguate internal wasm symbols when the same js_name
   199	/// appears in different namespaces. `__` is used as the separator because
   200	/// double underscores are unlikely to appear in user-defined names.
   201	pub fn qualified_name(js_namespace: Option<&[impl AsRef<str>]>, js_name: &str) -> String {
   202	    match js_namespace {
   203	        Some(ns) if !ns.is_empty() => {
   204	            let mut name = ns
   205	                .iter()
   206	                .map(|s| s.as_ref())
   207	                .collect::<alloc::vec::Vec<_>>()
   208	                .join("__");
   209	            name.push_str("__");
   210	            name.push_str(js_name);
   211	            name
   212	        }
   213	        _ => js_name.to_string(),
   214	    }
   215	}
   216	
   217	pub fn new_function(struct_name: &str) -> String {
   218	    let mut name = "__wbg_".to_string();
   219	    name.extend(struct_name.chars().flat_map(|s| s.to_lowercase()));
   220	    name.push_str("_new");
   221	    name
   222	}
   223	
   224	pub fn free_function(struct_name: &str) -> String {
   225	    let mut name = "__wbg_".to_string();
   226	    name.extend(struct_name.chars().flat_map(|s| s.to_lowercase()));
   227	    name.push_str("_free");
   228	    name
   229	}
   230

   429	    /// Like `Setter`, but for class fields instead of instance fields.
   430	    ClassSetter(JsImport, String),
   431	}
   432	
   433	/// What can actually be imported and typically a value in each of the variants
   434	/// above of `AuxImport`
   435	///
   436	/// A `JsImport` is intended to indicate what exactly is being imported for a
   437	/// particular operation.
   438	#[derive(Debug, Hash, Eq, PartialEq, Clone)]
   439	pub struct JsImport {
   440	    /// The base of whatever is being imported, either from a module, the global
   441	    /// namespace, or similar.
   442	    pub name: JsImportName,
   443	    /// Various field accesses (like `.foo.bar.baz`) to hang off the `name`
   444	    /// above.
   445	    pub fields: Vec<String>,
   446	}
   447	
   448	/// Return value of `determine_import` which is where we look at an imported
   449	/// function AST and figure out where it's actually being imported from
   450	/// (performing some validation checks and whatnot).
   451	#[derive(Debug, Hash, Eq, PartialEq, Clone)]
   452	pub enum JsImportName {
   453	    /// An item is imported from the global scope. The `name` is what's
   454	    /// imported.
   455	    Global { name: String },
   456	    /// Same as `Global`, except the `name` is imported via an ESM import from
   457	    /// the specified `module` path.
   458	    Module { module: String, name: String },
   459	    /// Same as `Module`, except we're importing from a local module defined in
   460	    /// a local JS snippet.
   461	    LocalModule { module: String, name: String },
   462	    /// Same as `Module`, except we're importing from an `inline_js` attribute
   463	    InlineJs {
   464	        unique_crate_identifier: String,
   465	        snippet_idx_in_crate: usize,
   466	        name: String,
   467	    },
   468	    /// A global import which may have a number of vendor prefixes associated
   469	    /// with it, like `webkitAudioPrefix`. The `name` is the name to test
   470	    /// whether it's prefixed.
   471	    VendorPrefixed { name: String, prefixes: Vec<String> },
   472	}
   473	
   474	impl walrus::CustomSection for WasmBindgenAux {
   475	    fn name(&self) -> &str {

   130	/// The possible types of module to import from
   131	#[cfg_attr(feature = "extra-traits", derive(Debug))]
   132	#[derive(Clone)]
   133	pub enum ImportModule {
   134	    /// Import from the named module, with relative paths interpreted
   135	    Named(String, Span),
   136	    /// Import from the named module, without interpreting paths
   137	    RawNamed(String, Span),
   138	    /// Import from an inline JS snippet
   139	    Inline(usize),
   140	}
   141	
   142	impl Hash for ImportModule {
   143	    fn hash<H: Hasher>(&self, h: &mut H) {
   144	        match self {
   145	            ImportModule::Named(name, _) => (1u8, name).hash(h),
   146	            ImportModule::Inline(idx) => (2u8, idx).hash(h),
   147	            ImportModule::RawNamed(name, _) => (3u8, name).hash(h),
   148	        }
   149	    }
   150	}

   253	
   254	fn shared_enum<'a>(e: &'a ast::Enum, intern: &'a Interner) -> Enum<'a> {
   255	    Enum {
   256	        name: &e.js_name,
   257	        signed: e.signed,
   258	        variants: e
   259	            .variants
   260	            .iter()
   261	            .map(|v| shared_variant(v, intern))
   262	            .collect(),
   263	        comments: e.comments.iter().map(|s| &**s).collect(),
   264	        generate_typescript: e.generate_typescript,
   265	        js_namespace: e
   266	            .js_namespace
   267	            .as_ref()
   268	            .map(|ns| ns.iter().map(|s| &**s).collect()),
   269	        private: e.private,
   270	    }
   271	}
   272	
   273	fn shared_variant<'a>(v: &'a ast::Variant, intern: &'a Interner) -> EnumVariant<'a> {
   274	    EnumVariant {
   275	        name: intern.intern(&v.name),
   276	        value: v.value,
   277	        comments: v.comments.iter().map(|s| &**s).collect(),
   278	    }
   279	}
   280	
   281	fn shared_import<'a>(i: &'a ast::Import, intern: &'a Interner) -> Result<Import<'a>, Diagnostic> {
   282	    // Resolve reexport name: use explicit rename if provided, otherwise use the import's name
   283	    let reexport = i.reexport.as_ref().map(|rename_opt| {
   284	        rename_opt.clone().unwrap_or_else(|| {
   285	            // Get the default name from the import kind
   286	            match &i.kind {
   287	                ast::ImportKind::Type(t) => t.js_name.clone(),
   288	                ast::ImportKind::Function(f) => f.function.name.clone(),
   289	                ast::ImportKind::Static(s) => s.js_name.clone(),
   290	                _ => unreachable!("reexport only supported on types, functions, and statics"),
   291	            }
   292	        })
   293	    });
   294	
   295	    Ok(Import {
   296	        module: i
   297	            .module
   298	            .as_ref()
   299	            .map(|m| shared_module(m, intern, false))
   300	            .transpose()?,
   301	        js_namespace: i.js_namespace.clone(),
   302	        reexport,
   303	        kind: shared_import_kind(&i.kind, intern)?,
   304	    })
   305	}
   306	
   307	fn shared_lit_or_expr<'a>(i: &'a ast::LitOrExpr, _intern: &'a Interner) -> LitOrExpr<'a> {
   308	    match i {
   309	        ast::LitOrExpr::Lit(lit) => LitOrExpr::Lit(lit),
   310	        ast::LitOrExpr::Expr(expr) => LitOrExpr::Expr(expr),
   311	    }
   312	}

    39	        get(data) != 0
    40	    }
    41	}

    43	impl<'src> Decode<'src> for u32 {
    44	    fn decode(data: &mut &'src [u8]) -> Self {
    45	        let mut cur = 0;
    46	        let mut offset = 0;
    47	        loop {
    48	            let byte = get(data);
    49	            cur |= ((byte & 0x7f) as u32) << offset;
    50	            if byte & 0x80 == 0 {
    51	                break cur;
    52	            }
    53	            offset += 7;
    54	        }
    55	    }
    56	}
    57	
    58	impl<'src> Decode<'src> for &'src str {
    59	    fn decode(data: &mut &'src [u8]) -> &'src str {
    60	        let n = u32::decode(data);
    61	        let (a, b) = data.split_at(n as usize);
    62	        *data = b;
    63	        let r = str::from_utf8(a).unwrap();
    64	        log::trace!("decoded string {r:?}");
    65	        r
    66	    }
    67	}

  1986	    js_namespace: Option<JsNamespace>,

  1988	
  1989	impl MacroParse<ForeignItemCtx> for syn::ForeignItem {
  1990	    fn macro_parse(
  1991	        mut self,
  1992	        program: &mut ast::Program,
  1993	        ctx: ForeignItemCtx,
  1994	    ) -> Result<(), Diagnostic> {
  1995	        let item_opts = {
  1996	            let attrs = match self {
  1997	                syn::ForeignItem::Fn(ref mut f) => &mut f.attrs,
  1998	                syn::ForeignItem::Type(ref mut t) => &mut t.attrs,
  1999	                syn::ForeignItem::Static(ref mut s) => &mut s.attrs,
  2000	                syn::ForeignItem::Verbatim(v) => {
  2001	                    let mut item: syn::ItemStatic =
  2002	                        syn::parse(v.into()).expect("only foreign functions/types allowed for now");
  2003	                    let item_opts = BindgenAttrs::find(&mut item.attrs)?;
  2004	                    let reexport = item_opts.reexport().cloned();
  2005	                    let kind = item.convert((program, item_opts, &ctx.module))?;
  2006	
  2007	                    program.imports.push(ast::Import {
  2008	                        module: None,
  2009	                        js_namespace: None,
  2010	                        reexport,
  2011	                        kind,
  2012	                    });
  2013	
  2014	                    return Ok(());
  2015	                }
  2016	                _ => panic!("only foreign functions/types allowed for now"),
  2017	            };
  2018	            BindgenAttrs::find(attrs)?
  2019	        };
  2020	
  2021	        let js_namespace = item_opts
  2022	            .js_namespace()
  2023	            .map(|(s, _)| s)
  2024	            .or(ctx.js_namespace)
  2025	            .map(|s| s.0);
  2026	        let module = ctx.module;
  2027	        let reexport = item_opts.reexport().cloned();
  2028	
  2029	        let kind = match self {
  2030	            syn::ForeignItem::Fn(f) => f.convert((program, item_opts, &module))?,
  2031	            syn::ForeignItem::Type(t) => t.convert((program, item_opts))?,
  2032	            syn::ForeignItem::Static(s) => s.convert((program, item_opts, &module))?,
  2033	            _ => panic!("only foreign functions/types allowed for now"),
  2034	        };
  2035	
  2036	        // check for JS keywords
  2037	
  2038	        // We only need to check if there isn't a JS namespace or module. If
  2039	        // there is namespace, then we already checked the namespace while
  2040	        // parsing. If there is a module, we can rename the import symbol to
  2041	        // avoid using keywords.
  2042	        let needs_check = js_namespace.is_none() && module.is_none();
  2043	        if needs_check {
  2044	            match &kind {
  2045	                ast::ImportKind::Function(import_function) => {
  2046	                    if matches!(import_function.kind, ast::ImportFunctionKind::Normal)
  2047	                        && is_non_value_js_keyword(&import_function.function.name)
  2048	                    {
  2049	                        bail_span!(
  2050	                            import_function.rust_name,
  2051	                            "Imported function cannot use the JS keyword `{}` as its name.",
  2052	                            import_function.function.name
  2053	                        );
  2054	                    }
  2055	                }
  2056	                ast::ImportKind::Static(import_static) => {
  2057	                    if is_non_value_js_keyword(&import_static.js_name) {
  2058	                        bail_span!(
  2059	                            import_static.rust_name,
  2060	                            "Imported static cannot use the JS keyword `{}` as its name.",
  2061	                            import_static.js_name
  2062	                        );
  2063	                    }
  2064	                }
  2065	                ast::ImportKind::String(_) => {
  2066	                    // static strings don't have JS names, so we don't need to check for JS keywords
  2067	                }
  2068	                ast::ImportKind::Type(import_type) => {
  2069	                    if is_non_value_js_keyword(&import_type.js_name) {
  2070	                        bail_span!(
  2071	                            import_type.rust_name,
  2072	                            "Imported type cannot use the JS keyword `{}` as its name.",
  2073	                            import_type.js_name
  2074	                        );
  2075	                    }
  2076	                }
  2077	                ast::ImportKind::Enum(_) => {
  2078	                    // string enums aren't possible here
  2079	                }
  2080	            }
  2081	        }
  2082	
  2083	        program.imports.push(ast::Import {
  2084	            module,
  2085	            js_namespace,
  2086	            reexport,
  2087	            kind,
  2088	        });
  2089	
  2090	        Ok(())
  2091	    }
  2092	}
  2093	
  2094	pub fn module_from_opts(
  2095	    program: &mut ast::Program,
  2096	    opts: &BindgenAttrs,
  2097	) -> Result<Option<ast::ImportModule>, Diagnostic> {
  2098	    if let Some(path) = opts.wasm_bindgen() {
  2099	        program.wasm_bindgen = path.clone();
  2100	    }

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/crates/cli/tests/wasm-bindgen/reference.rs:
     1	//! A test suite to check the reference JS and Wasm output of the `wasm-bindgen`
     2	//! library.
     3	//!
     4	//! This is intended as an end-to-end integration test where we can track
     5	//! changes to the JS and Wasm output.
     6	//!
     7	//! Tests are located in `reference/*.rs` files and are accompanied with sibling
     8	//! `*.js` files and `*.wat` files with the expected output of the `*.rs`
     9	//! compilation. Use `BLESS=1` in the environment to automatically update all
    10	//! tests.
    11	//!
    12	//! ## Dependencies
    13	//!
    14	//! By default, tests only have access to the `wasm-bindgen` and
    15	//! `wasm-bindgen-futures` crates. Additional crates can be used by declaring
    16	//! them as dependencies using a comment at the top of the test file.
    17	//! For example:
    18	//!
    19	//! ```rust
    20	//! // DEPENDENCY: web-sys = { path = '{root}/crates/web-sys', features = ['console', 'Url', 'MediaSourceReadyState'] }
    21	//! ```
    22	//!
    23	//! This will add the `web-sys` crate as a dependency to the test, allowing the
    24	//! test to use the `console`, `Url`, and `MediaSourceReadyState` features, as
    25	//! well as the `web-sys` crate itself.
    26	//!
    27	//! Note that the `{root}` placeholder will be replaced with the path to the
    28	//! root of the `wasm-bindgen` repository.
    29	//!
    30	//! Multiple dependencies can be declared in a single test file using multiple
    31	//! `DEPENDENCY:` comments.
    32	//!
    33	//! ## Custom CLI flags
    34	//!
    35	//! By default, tests will use the `bundler` target. Custom CLI flags can be
    36	//! passed to the `wasm-bindgen` CLI by declaring them in a comment at the top
    37	//! of the test file. For example:
    38	//!
    39	//! ```rust
    40	//! // FLAGS: --target=web --reference-types
    41	//! ```
    42	//!
    43	//! Multiple comments can be used to run the test multiple times with different
    44	//! flags.
    45	//!
    46	//! ```rust
    47	//! // FLAGS: --target=web
    48	//! // FLAGS: --target=nodejs
    49	//! ```
    50	
    51	use crate::Project;
    52	use anyhow::Result;
    53	use assert_cmd::Command;
    54	use regex::Regex;
    55	use std::borrow::Cow;
    56	use std::collections::BTreeMap;
    57	use std::collections::HashMap;
    58	use std::env;
    59	use std::fs;
    60	use std::path::{Path, PathBuf};
    61	use std::sync::LazyLock;
    62	use walrus::{
    63	    ElementItems, ElementKind, ExportItem, FunctionKind, ImportKind, Module, ModuleConfig,
    64	};
    65	
    66	macro_rules! regex {
    67	    ($re:literal) => {{
    68	        static RE: LazyLock<Regex> = LazyLock::new(|| Regex::new($re).unwrap());
    69	        &*RE
    70	    }};
    71	}
    72	
    73	// A helper to remove unstable parts of the output like function indices
    74	// and hash values, while ensuring that the replacement names stay consistent
    75	// between all output files.
    76	#[derive(Default)]
    77	struct Sanitizer {
    78	    prev_replacements: HashMap<String, usize>,
    79	}
    80	
    81	impl Sanitizer {
    82	    fn sanitize_one<'s>(
    83	        &mut self,
    84	        s: &'s str,
    85	        regex: &Regex,
    86	        replacement: impl Fn(usize) -> String,
    87	    ) -> Cow<'s, str> {
    88	        regex.replace_all(s, |caps: &regex::Captures| {
    89	            let index = self.prev_replacements.len();
    90	
    91	            let index = self
    92	                .prev_replacements
    93	                .entry(caps[0].to_string())
    94	                .or_insert(index);
    95	
    96	            replacement(*index)
    97	        })
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    fn sanitize(&mut self, s: &str) -> String {
   101	        // Cast descriptors for closures contain unstable function indices, so we need to sanitize the hash.
   102	        let s = self.sanitize_one(s, regex!(r"__wbindgen_cast_[0-9a-f]{16}"), |idx| {
   103	            format!("__wbindgen_cast_{idx:016x}")
   104	        });
   105	
   106	        // `h...` are mangled generic function names with unstable type IDs.
   107	        let s = self.sanitize_one(&s, regex!(r"h[0-9a-f]{16}"), |idx| format!("h{idx:016x}"));
   108	
   109	        // Cast descriptors contain `Closure`'s `Debug` impl which has unstable function indices.
   110	        let s = self.sanitize_one(&s, regex!(r"_idx: \d+,"), |idx| format!("_idx: {idx},"));
   111	
   112	        s.into_owned()
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    fn assert_same(&mut self, output: &str, expected: &Path) -> Result<()> {
   116	        let output = self.sanitize(output);
   117	        if env::var("BLESS").is_ok() {
   118	            fs::write(expected, output.as_bytes())?;
   119	        } else {
   120	            let expected = fs::read_to_string(expected)?;
   121	            pretty_assertions::assert_str_eq!(expected, output);
   122	        }
   123	        Ok(())
   124	    }
   125	}
   126	
   127	#[rstest::rstest]
   128	fn runtest(
   129	    #[base_dir = "tests/reference"]
   130	    #[files("*.rs")]
   131	    test: PathBuf,
   132	) -> Result<()> {
   133	    runtest_with_opts(test, None, |_| ())
   134	}

   137	fn runtest_targets_atomics() -> Result<()> {
   138	    let mut test = PathBuf::from(env!("CARGO_MANIFEST_DIR"));
   139	    test.push("tests");
   140	    test.push("reference");
   141	    test.push("targets.rs");
   142	
   143	    runtest_with_opts(test, Some("atomics"), |command| {
   144	        command
   145	            .env("RUSTUP_TOOLCHAIN", "nightly")
   146	            .env(
   147	                "RUSTFLAGS",
   148	                "-Ctarget-feature=+atomics \
   149	                -Clink-args=--shared-memory \
   150	                -Clink-args=--max-memory=1073741824 \
   151	                -Clink-args=--import-memory \
   152	                -Clink-args=--export=__wasm_init_tls \
   153	                -Clink-args=--export=__tls_size \
   154	                -Clink-args=--export=__tls_align \
   155	                -Clink-args=--export=__tls_base",
   156	            )
   157	            .arg("-Zbuild-std=std,panic_abort");
   158	    })
   159	}

   161	#[test]
   162	fn no_duplicate_wasm_export_in_node_esm_atomics_debug() -> Result<()> {
   163	    let mut test = PathBuf::from(env!("CARGO_MANIFEST_DIR"));
   164	    test.push("tests");
   165	    test.push("reference");
   166	    test.push("targets.rs");
   167	
   168	    let mut project = Project::new("targets_reftest_atomics_debug_no_duplicate_wasm_export");
   169	    project.dep("wasm-bindgen-futures = { path = '{root}/crates/futures' }");
   170	    project
   171	        .cargo_cmd
   172	        .env("RUSTUP_TOOLCHAIN", "nightly")
   173	        .env(
   174	            "RUSTFLAGS",
   175	            "-Ctarget-feature=+atomics \
   176	            -Clink-args=--shared-memory \
   177	            -Clink-args=--max-memory=1073741824 \
   178	            -Clink-args=--import-memory \
   179	            -Clink-args=--export=__wasm_init_tls \
   180	            -Clink-args=--export=__tls_size \
   181	            -Clink-args=--export=__tls_align \
   182	            -Clink-args=--export=__tls_base",
   183	        )
   184	        .arg("-Zbuild-std=std,panic_abort");
   185	    project.file_link("src/lib.rs", &test);
   186	
   187	    let out_dir = project
   188	        .wasm_bindgen("--target=experimental-nodejs-module --debug --out-name reference_test")?;
   189	    let js = fs::read_to_string(out_dir.join("reference_test.js"))?;
   190	    let export_count = js.matches("export { wasm as __wasm").count();
   191	    assert_eq!(
   192	        export_count, 1,
   193	        "expected exactly one ESM __wasm export, found {export_count}"
   194	    );
   195	    Ok(())
   196	}

   887	    ) -> Result<Self::Target, Diagnostic> {
   888	        if let syn::StaticMutability::Mut(_) = self.mutability {
   889	            bail_span!(self.mutability, "cannot import mutable globals yet")
   890	        }
   891	
   892	        if let Some(span) = opts.static_string() {
   893	            return Err(Diagnostic::span_error(
   894	                *span,
   895	                "static strings require a string literal",
   896	            ));
   897	        }
   898	
   899	        let default_name = self.ident.to_string();
   900	        let js_name = opts
   901	            .js_name()
   902	            .map(|p| p.0)
   903	            .unwrap_or(&default_name)
   904	            .to_string();
   905	        let shim = format!(
   906	            "__wbg_static_accessor_{}_{}",
   907	            self.ident,
   908	            ShortHash((&js_name, module, &self.ident)),
   909	        );
   910	        let thread_local = opts.get_thread_local()?;
   911	
   912	        opts.check_used();
   913	        Ok(ast::ImportKind::Static(ast::ImportStatic {
   914	            ty: *self.ty,
   915	            vis: self.vis,
   916	            rust_name: self.ident.clone(),
   917	            js_name,
   918	            shim: Ident::new(&shim, Span::call_site()),
   919	            wasm_bindgen: program.wasm_bindgen.clone(),
   920	            thread_local,
   921	        }))
   922	    }
   923	}

   933	impl TryToTokens for ast::ImportKind {
   934	    fn try_to_tokens(&self, tokens: &mut TokenStream) -> Result<(), Diagnostic> {
   935	        match *self {
   936	            ast::ImportKind::Function(ref f) => f.try_to_tokens(tokens)?,
   937	            ast::ImportKind::Static(ref s) => s.to_tokens(tokens),
   938	            ast::ImportKind::String(ref s) => s.to_tokens(tokens),
   939	            ast::ImportKind::Type(ref t) => t.try_to_tokens(tokens)?,
   940	            ast::ImportKind::Enum(ref e) => e.to_tokens(tokens),
   941	        }
   942	
   943	        Ok(())
   944	    }
   945	}

   947	impl TryToTokens for ast::ImportType {
   948	    fn try_to_tokens(&self, tokens: &mut TokenStream) -> Result<(), Diagnostic> {
   949	        let vis = &self.vis;
   950	        let rust_name = &self.rust_name;
   951	        let attrs = &self.attrs;
   952	        let doc_comment = match &self.doc_comment {
   953	            None => "",
   954	            Some(comment) => comment,
   955	        };
   956	        let instanceof_shim = Ident::new(&self.instanceof_shim, Span::call_site());
   957

   959	        let internal_obj = match self.extends.first() {
   960	            Some(target) => {
   961	                quote! { #target }
   962	            }
   963	            None => {
   964	                quote! { #wasm_bindgen::JsValue }
   965	            }
   966	        };

   979	                JsValue::describe()
   980	            }
   981	        };

   984	            quote! {
   985	                #[inline]
   986	                fn is_type_of(val: &JsValue) -> bool {

   135	        fn enforce_used(self) -> Result<(), Diagnostic> {
   136	            // Account for the fact this method was called
   137	            ATTRS.with(|state| state.checks.set(state.checks.get() + 1));
   138	
   139	            let mut errors = Vec::new();
   140	            for (used, attr) in self.attrs.iter() {
   141	                if used.get() {
   142	                    continue
   143	                }
   144	                let span = match attr {
   145	                    $(BindgenAttr::$variant(span, ..) => span,)*
   146	                };
   147	                errors.push(Diagnostic::span_error(*span, "unused wasm_bindgen attribute"));
   148	            }
   149	            Diagnostic::from_vec(errors)
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        fn check_used(self) {
   153	            // Account for the fact this method was called

    #[wasm_bindgen(reexport, js_name = "LanguageCode", skip_typescript)]
    fn __helper_language_code();
}

#[wasm_bindgen]
pub fn touch() {}
RS

  echo "BUG: LanguageCode found in generated TypeScript" >&2
  exit 1
fi
EOF

  1853	    fn write_exports(&mut self) -> Result<(), Error> {
  1854	        let exports = std::mem::take(&mut self.exports);
  1855	        for (ref export_name, export) in exports {
  1856	            match export {
  1857	                ExportEntry::Definition(def) => {
  1858	                    self.export_name_list.push(export_name.clone());
  1859	                    self.export_def(Some(export_name), &def);
  1860	                }

  1863	                        Some(id) => (id, true),
  1864	                        None => (self.generate_identifier(export_name), false),
  1865	                    };

  1870	                        String::new()
  1871	                    };

  1873	                        format!("const {identifier} = {{}};\n{ns_dst}")
  1874	                    } else {
  1875	                        self.global(&ns_dst);
  1876	                        "".to_string()
  1877	                    };

  1888	                        },

  1926	    fn write_namespace_ts(
  1927	        namespace: &BTreeMap<String, ExportEntry>,
  1928	        indent: &str,
  1929	    ) -> Result<String, Error> {
  1930	        let mut ts_dst = String::from("{\n");
  1931	        for (name, entry) in namespace {
  1932	            let indent = format!("  {indent}");
  1933	            let entry_ts = match entry {
  1934	                ExportEntry::Namespace(ns) => Self::write_namespace_ts(&ns.ns, &indent)?,
  1935	                ExportEntry::Definition(def) => format!("typeof {}", def.identifier),
  1936	            };
  1937	            if is_valid_ident(name) {
  1938	                ts_dst.push_str(&format!("{indent}{name}: {entry_ts},\n"));
  1939	            } else {
  1940	                ts_dst.push_str(&format!("{indent}'{name}': {entry_ts},\n"));
  1941	            }
  1942	        }
  1943	        ts_dst.push_str(&format!("{indent}}}"));
  1944	        Ok(ts_dst)
  1945	    }
  1946	
  1947	    fn expose_drop_ref(&mut self) {
  1948	        // Note that here we check if `idx` shouldn't actually be dropped. This
  1949	        // is due to the fact that `JsValue::null()` and friends can be passed
  1950	        // by value to JS where we'll automatically call this method. Those
  1951	        // constants, however, cannot be dropped. See #1054 for removing this
  1952	        // branch.
  1953	        //
  1954	        // Otherwise the free operation here is pretty simple, just appending to
  1955	        // the linked list of heap slots that are free.
  1956	        self.expose_global_heap();
  1957	        self.expose_global_heap_next();
  1958	        self.intrinsic(
  1959	            "drop_ref".into(),
  1960	            "dropObject".into(),
  1961	            format!(
  1962	                "
  1963	                function dropObject(idx) {{
  1964	                    if (idx < {}) return;
  1965	                    heap[idx] = heap_next;
  1966	                    heap_next = idx;
  1967	                }}
  1968	                ",
  1969	                INITIAL_HEAP_OFFSET + INITIAL_HEAP_VALUES.len(),
  1970	            )
  1971	            .into(),
  1972	        );
  1973	    }
  1974	
  1975	    fn expose_global_heap(&mut self) {
  1976	        assert!(!self.config.externref);
  1977	        if matches!(self.config.mode, OutputMode::Emscripten) {
  1978	            self.emscripten_global_deps.insert("heap".to_string());
  1979	            return;
  1980	        }
  1981	        self.intrinsic(
  1982	            "heap".into(),
  1983	            None,
  1984	            format!(
  1985	                "
  1986	                let heap = new Array({INITIAL_HEAP_OFFSET}).fill(undefined);
  1987	                heap.push({});
  1988	                ",
  1989	                INITIAL_HEAP_VALUES.join(", ")
  1990	            )
  1991	            .into(),
  1992	        );
  1993	    }

  5631	/// Defines an export with an optional namespace path segment
  5632	/// Namespaces are defined into the exports map as needed via ExportEntry::Namespace
  5633	fn define_export(
  5634	    exports: &mut BTreeMap<String, ExportEntry>,
  5635	    export_name: &str,
  5636	    ns_path: &[String],
  5637	    export: ExportEntry,
  5638	) -> Result<(), Error> {
  5639	    // Namespaces are only defined into exports by this function, not by consumers of this function.
  5640	    assert!(!matches!(export, ExportEntry::Namespace(_)));
  5641	
  5642	    if ns_path.is_empty() {
  5643	        match exports.entry(export_name.to_string()) {
  5644	            Entry::Vacant(e) => {
  5645	                e.insert(export);
  5646	            }
  5647	            Entry::Occupied(mut e) => {
  5648	                if let ExportEntry::Definition(def) = export {
  5649	                    if def.definition.is_empty() {
  5650	                        if let ExportEntry::Namespace(ns) = e.get_mut() {
  5651	                            if ns.id.is_none() {
  5652	                                ns.id = Some(def.identifier);
  5653	                                return Ok(());
  5654	                            }
  5655	                        }
  5656	                    }
  5657	                }
  5658	                bail!("Cannot define export over existing namespace {export_name}");
  5659	            }
  5660	        };
  5661	    } else {
  5662	        let export_entry = exports
  5663	            .entry(ns_path[0].to_string())
  5664	            .or_insert(ExportEntry::Namespace(Default::default()));
  5665	        let ns = match export_entry {
  5666	            ExportEntry::Namespace(ns) => ns,
  5667	            ExportEntry::Definition(def) if def.definition.is_empty() => {
  5668	                *export_entry = ExportEntry::Namespace(ExportedNamespace {
  5669	                    id: Some(def.identifier.to_string()),
  5670	                    ns: BTreeMap::new(),
  5671	                });
  5672	                let ExportEntry::Namespace(ns) = export_entry else {
  5673	                    unreachable!();
  5674	                };
  5675	                ns
  5676	            }
  5677	            _ => {
  5678	                bail!("Cannot to define namespace export over existing definition {export_name}");
  5679	            }
  5680	        };
  5681	        define_export(&mut ns.ns, export_name, &ns_path[1..], export)?;
  5682	    }
  5683	    Ok(())
  5684	}

#!/usr/bin/env bash

[package]
name = "repro_reexport_no_skip"
version = "0.1.0"
edition = "2021"

[lib]
crate-type = ["cdylib"]

[dependencies]
wasm-bindgen = { path = "$ROOT" }
TOML

use wasm_bindgen::prelude::*;
#[wasm_bindgen(module = "my-codes")]
extern "C" {
    #[wasm_bindgen(reexport, js_name = "LanguageCode")]
    fn __helper_language_code();
}
#[wasm_bindgen]
pub fn touch() {}
RS

"$ROOT/target/debug/wasm-bindgen" "$WORK/target/wasm32-unknown-unknown/debug/repro_reexport_no_skip.wasm" --out-dir "$WORK/out" --target bundler --typescript
cat "$WORK/out/repro_reexport_no_skip.d.ts"

EOF

+ const CLOSURE_DTORS = (typeof FinalizationRegistry === 'undefined')
+     ? { register: () => {}, unregister: () => {} }
+     : new FinalizationRegistry(state => wasm.__wbindgen_destroy_closure(state.a, state.b));

+ function debugString(val) {
+     // primitive types
+     const type = typeof val;
+     if (type == 'number' || type == 'boolean' || val == null) {
+         return  `${val}`;
+     }
+     if (type == 'string') {
+         return `"${val}"`;
+     }
+     if (type == 'symbol') {
+         const description = val.description;
+         if (description == null) {
+             return 'Symbol';
+         } else {
+             return `Symbol(${description})`;
+         }
+     }
+     if (type == 'function') {
+         const name = val.name;
+         if (typeof name == 'string' && name.length > 0) {
+             return `Function(${name})`;
+         } else {
+             return 'Function';
+         }
+     }
+     // objects
+     if (Array.isArray(val)) {
+         const length = val.length;
+         let debug = '[';
+         if (length > 0) {
+             debug += debugString(val[0]);
+         }
+         for(let i = 1; i < length; i++) {
+             debug += ', ' + debugString(val[i]);
+         }
+         debug += ']';
+         return debug;
+     }
+     // Test for built-in
+     const builtInMatches = /\[object ([^\]]+)\]/.exec(toString.call(val));
+     let className;
+     if (builtInMatches && builtInMatches.length > 1) {
+         className = builtInMatches[1];
+     } else {
+         // Failed to match the standard '[object ClassName]'
+         return toString.call(val);
+     }
+     if (className == 'Object') {
+         // we're a user defined class or Object
+         // JSON.stringify avoids problems with cycles, and is generally much
+         // easier than looping through ownProperties of `val`.
+         try {
+             return 'Object(' + JSON.stringify(val) + ')';
+         } catch (_) {
+             return 'Object';
+         }
+     }
+     // errors
+     if (val instanceof Error) {
+         return `${val.name}: ${val.message}\n${val.stack}`;
+     }
+     // TODO we could test for more things here, like `Set`s and `Map`s.
+     return className;
+ }
+

+ function makeMutClosure(arg0, arg1, f) {
+     const state = { a: arg0, b: arg1, cnt: 1 };
+     const real = (...args) => {
+ 
+         // First up with a closure we increment the internal reference
+         // count. This ensures that the Rust closure environment won't
+         // be deallocated while we're invoking it.
+         state.cnt++;
+         const a = state.a;
+         state.a = 0;
+         try {

+         } finally {
+             state.a = a;
+             real._wbg_cb_unref();
+         }
+     };

+             CLOSURE_DTORS.unregister(state);
+         }
+     };
+     CLOSURE_DTORS.register(real, state, state);
+     return real;
+ }

+ function debugString(val) {
+     // primitive types
+     const type = typeof val;
+     if (type == 'number' || type == 'boolean' || val == null) {
+         return  `${val}`;
+     }
+     if (type == 'string') {
+         return `"${val}"`;
+     }
+     if (type == 'symbol') {
+         const description = val.description;
+         if (description == null) {
+             return 'Symbol';
+         } else {
+             return `Symbol(${description})`;
+         }
+     }
+     if (type == 'function') {
+         const name = val.name;
+         if (typeof name == 'string' && name.length > 0) {
+             return `Function(${name})`;
+         } else {
+             return 'Function';
+         }
+     }
+     // objects
+     if (Array.isArray(val)) {
+         const length = val.length;
+         let debug = '[';
+         if (length > 0) {
+             debug += debugString(val[0]);
+         }
+         for(let i = 1; i < length; i++) {
+             debug += ', ' + debugString(val[i]);
+         }
+         debug += ']';
+         return debug;
+     }
+     // Test for built-in
+     const builtInMatches = /\[object ([^\]]+)\]/.exec(toString.call(val));
+     let className;
+     if (builtInMatches && builtInMatches.length > 1) {
+         className = builtInMatches[1];
+     } else {
+         // Failed to match the standard '[object ClassName]'
+         return toString.call(val);
+     }
+     if (className == 'Object') {
+         // we're a user defined class or Object
+         // JSON.stringify avoids problems with cycles, and is generally much
+         // easier than looping through ownProperties of `val`.
+         try {
+             return 'Object(' + JSON.stringify(val) + ')';
+         } catch (_) {
+             return 'Object';
+         }
+     }
+     // errors
+     if (val instanceof Error) {
+         return `${val.name}: ${val.message}\n${val.stack}`;
+     }
+     // TODO we could test for more things here, like `Set`s and `Map`s.
+     return className;
+ }

+ function makeMutClosure(arg0, arg1, f) {
+     const state = { a: arg0, b: arg1, cnt: 1 };
+     const real = (...args) => {
+

+         // count. This ensures that the Rust closure environment won't
+         // be deallocated while we're invoking it.
+         state.cnt++;
+         const a = state.a;
+         state.a = 0;
+         try {
+             return f(a, state.b, ...args);
+         } finally {
+             state.a = a;
+             real._wbg_cb_unref();
+         }

+             state.a = 0;
+             CLOSURE_DTORS.unregister(state);
+         }
+     };
+     CLOSURE_DTORS.register(real, state, state);
+     return real;
+ }
